## CSS Style Change → Layout/Paint Chain in Firefox/Gecko

The chain spans **6 phases** across **10 C++ source files**:

### Phase 1 — Style Change Notification
**`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`**

`RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent()` (line 2383) is the public entry point. Called by DOM/CSSOM mutation paths (attribute changes, class changes, stylesheet mutations), it validates preconditions, sets `mHaveNonAnimationRestyles`, and calls `Servo_NoteExplicitHints()` to record the restyle hint on the element in the Servo style engine. No styles are recomputed yet — the element is merely queued.

### Phase 2 — Frame Style Recomputation
**`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`**

After traversal, `ProcessPostTraversal()` walks the restyle root subtree applying computed styles to frames and collecting an `nsStyleChangeList`. `ProcessRestyledFrames()` (line 1548) then iterates the change list, applying each `nsChangeHint` (frame reconstruction, geometry updates, reflow scheduling, repaint).
